                        </p>
                    </div>

                    {hasFinancialAccess && (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                            <div className="bg-white/10 backdrop-blur rounded-lg p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs text-blue-200">Projected Monthly</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-bold">
                                    {formatCurrency(analytics.monthlyProjection.projectedTotal)}
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-white/10 backdrop-blur rounded-lg p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs text-blue-200">Confidence</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-bold">
                                    {analytics.predictions.confidence.toFixed(0)}%
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-white/10 backdrop-blur rounded-lg p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs text-blue-200">Optimization Potential</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-bold text-green-300">
                                    +{formatCurrency(analytics.optimizationPotential.improvementAmount)}
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-white/10 backdrop-blur rounded-lg p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs text-blue-200">Fleet Score</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-bold">
                                    {Statistics.mean(analytics.carPerformance.map(c => c.totalScore)).toFixed(0)}/100
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* ================================================================
          KEY INSIGHTS CARDS
      ================================================================ */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                {analytics.insights.slice(0, 6).map((insight, index) => (
                    <InsightCard key={index} insight={insight} />
                ))}
            </div>

            {/* ================================================================
          TAB NAVIGATION
      ================================================================ */}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="flex overflow-x-auto border-b border-gray-200">
                    {[
                        { key: 'overview', label: 'Overview', icon: BarChart3 },
                        { key: 'predictions', label: 'Predictions', icon: TrendingUp },
                        { key: 'anomalies', label: 'Anomalies', icon: AlertTriangle },
                        { key: 'cars', label: 'Car Performance', icon: Truck },
                        { key: 'optimization', label: 'Optimization', icon: Zap }
                    ].map(({ key, label, icon: Icon }) => (
                        <button
                            key={key}
                            onClick={() => setActiveInsightTab(key)}
                            className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-4 sm:px-6 py-3 sm:py-4 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap ${activeInsightTab === key
                                    ? 'border-blue-600 text-blue-600 bg-blue-50'
                                    : 'border-transparent text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900 hover:bg-gray-50'
                                }`}
                        >
                            <Icon className="w-4 h-4" />
                            <span>{label}</span>
                        </button>
                    ))}
                </div>

                <div className="p-4 sm:p-6">
                    {/* OVERVIEW TAB */}
                    {activeInsightTab === 'overview' && (
                        <OverviewTab
                            analytics={analytics}
                            hasFinancialAccess={hasFinancialAccess}
                            formatCurrency={formatCurrency}
                            formatNumber={formatNumber}
                        />
                    )}

                    {/* PREDICTIONS TAB */}
                    {activeInsightTab === 'predictions' && hasFinancialAccess && (
                        <PredictionsTab
                            analytics={analytics}
                            statsByDate={statsByDate}
                            formatCurrency={formatCurrency}
                        />
                    )}

                    {/* ANOMALIES TAB */}
                    {activeInsightTab === 'anomalies' && (
                        <AnomaliesTab
                            analytics={analytics}
                            statsByDate={statsByDate}
                            hasFinancialAccess={hasFinancialAccess}
                            formatCurrency={formatCurrency}
                            formatNumber={formatNumber}
                        />
                    )}

                    {/* CAR PERFORMANCE TAB */}
                    {activeInsightTab === 'cars' && (
                        <CarPerformanceTab
                            analytics={analytics}
                            hasFinancialAccess={hasFinancialAccess}
                            formatCurrency={formatCurrency}
                            formatNumber={formatNumber}
                            selectedCar={selectedCar}
                            setSelectedCar={setSelectedCar}
                        />
                    )}

                    {/* OPTIMIZATION TAB */}
                    {activeInsightTab === 'optimization' && hasFinancialAccess && (
                        <OptimizationTab
                            analytics={analytics}
                            formatCurrency={formatCurrency}
                            formatNumber={formatNumber}
                        />
                    )}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// INSIGHT CARD COMPONENT
// ============================================================================

const InsightCard = ({ insight }) => {
    const typeStyles = {
        positive: {
            bg: 'bg-green-50',
            border: 'border-green-200',
            icon: 'bg-green-100 text-green-600',
            title: 'text-green-800'
        },
        warning: {
            bg: 'bg-amber-50',
            border: 'border-amber-200',
            icon: 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-600',
            title: 'text-amber-800'
        },
        info: {
            bg: 'bg-blue-50',
            border: 'border-blue-200',
            icon: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-600',
            title: 'text-blue-800'
        }
    };

    const style = typeStyles[insight.type] || typeStyles.info;
    const Icon = insight.type === 'positive' ? CheckCircle :
        insight.type === 'warning' ? AlertCircle : Lightbulb;

    return (
        <div className={`${style.bg} ${style.border} border rounded-lg p-4 hover:shadow-md transition-shadow`}>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
                <div className={`${style.icon} p-2 rounded-full h-fit`}>
                    <Icon className="w-5 h-5" />
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                        <h4 className={`font-semibold ${style.title}`}>{insight.title}</h4>
                        {insight.metric && (
                            <span className={`text-sm font-bold ${style.title} whitespace-nowrap`}>
                                {insight.metric}
                            </span>
                        )}
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">{insight.description}</p>
                    {insight.action && (
                        <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-2 flex items-center gap-1">
                            <Target className="w-3 h-3" />
                            {insight.action}
                        </p>
                    )}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// OVERVIEW TAB
// ============================================================================

const OverviewTab = ({ analytics, hasFinancialAccess, formatCurrency, formatNumber }) => {
    const { companyMetrics, predictions } = analytics;

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Company Comparison */}
            <div>
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Company Profitability Comparison</h3>
                <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                    <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
                        <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                            <tr>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Company</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Total Trips</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Volume (L)</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Distance (km)</th>
                                {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                    <>
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Revenue</th>
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">EGP/km</th>
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">EGP/L</th>
                                    </>
                                )}
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                            {companyMetrics.sort((a, b) => b.revenuePerKm - a.revenuePerKm).map((company, index) => (
                                <tr key={company.company} className={index === 0 ? 'bg-green-50' : ''}>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 flex items-center gap-2">
                                        {company.company}
                                        {index === 0 && <span className="text-xs bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">Top</span>}
                                    </td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{formatNumber(company.totalTrips)}</td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{formatNumber(company.totalVolume)}</td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{formatNumber(company.totalDistance)}</td>
                                    {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                        <>
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{formatCurrency(company.totalRevenue)}</td>
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 text-right">
                                                {formatNumber(company.revenuePerKm)}
                                            </td>
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{formatNumber(company.revenuePerLiter)}</td>
                                        </>
                                    )}
                                </tr>
                            ))}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Trend Summary */}
            {predictions?.insights && (
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                    <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-4">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                            {predictions.insights.trend === 'growing' ? (
                                <TrendingUp className="w-5 h-5 text-green-600" />
                            ) : predictions.insights.trend === 'declining' ? (
                                <TrendingDown className="w-5 h-5 text-red-600" />
                            ) : (
                                <Activity className="w-5 h-5 text-gray-600" />
                            )}
                            <span className="font-medium text-gray-900">Revenue Trend</span>
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                            {predictions.insights.trend === 'growing' ? '+' : ''}
                            {predictions.insights.trendStrength.toFixed(1)}%
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Period over period</p>
                    </div>

                    <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-4">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                            <Activity className="w-5 h-5 text-amber-600" />
                            <span className="font-medium text-gray-900">Volatility</span>
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                            {predictions.insights.volatility.toFixed(0)}%
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Daily variance</p>
                    </div>

                    <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-4">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                            <Target className="w-5 h-5 text-blue-600" />
                            <span className="font-medium text-gray-900">Forecast Confidence</span>
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                            {predictions.confidence.toFixed(0)}%
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Model accuracy</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// PREDICTIONS TAB
// ============================================================================

const PredictionsTab = ({ analytics, statsByDate, formatCurrency }) => {
    const { predictions, monthlyProjection } = analytics;

    // Combine historical and predicted data for chart
    const chartData = useMemo(() => {
        const historical = statsByDate.map(d => ({
            date: d.date,
            actual: d.total_revenue || 0,
            type: 'historical'
        }));

        const lastDate = new Date(statsByDate[statsByDate.length - 1]?.date || new Date());
        const predicted = predictions.predictions.map((p, i) => {
            const date = new Date(lastDate);
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + i + 1);
            return {
                date: date.toISOString().split('T')[0],
                predicted: p.predicted,
                lower: p.lower,
                upper: p.upper,
                type: 'forecast'
            };
        });

        return [...historical, ...predicted];
    }, [statsByDate, predictions]);

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Projection Summary */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                <div className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <p className="text-sm text-blue-600 font-medium">Current Total</p>
                    <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-900">
                        {formatCurrency(monthlyProjection.currentTotal)}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-blue-600">{statsByDate.length} days recorded</p>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <p className="text-sm text-green-600 font-medium">Projected Monthly</p>
                    <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-900">
                        {formatCurrency(monthlyProjection.projectedTotal)}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-600">30-day projection</p>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-purple-50 border border-purple-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <p className="text-sm text-purple-600 font-medium">Remaining Forecast</p>
                    <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-purple-900">
                        {formatCurrency(monthlyProjection.projectedRemaining)}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-purple-600">Next {30 - statsByDate.length} days</p>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 font-medium">Confidence Level</p>
                    <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                        {predictions.confidence.toFixed(0)}%
                    </p>
                    <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2 mt-2">
                        <div
                            className={`h-2 rounded-full ${predictions.confidence >= 70 ? 'bg-green-500' :
                                    predictions.confidence >= 50 ? 'bg-amber-500' : 'bg-red-500'
                                }`}
                            style={{ width: `${predictions.confidence}%` }}
                        />
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Forecast Chart */}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4">
                <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">30-Day Revenue Forecast</h4>
                <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={400}>
                    <AreaChart data={chartData}>
                        <defs>
                            <linearGradient id="actualGradient" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                                <stop offset="5%" stopColor="#3B82F6" stopOpacity={0.3} />
                                <stop offset="95%" stopColor="#3B82F6" stopOpacity={0} />
                            </linearGradient>
                            <linearGradient id="forecastGradient" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                                <stop offset="5%" stopColor="#10B981" stopOpacity={0.3} />
                                <stop offset="95%" stopColor="#10B981" stopOpacity={0} />
                            </linearGradient>
                        </defs>
                        <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#E5E7EB" />
                        <XAxis
                            dataKey="date"
                            tick={{ fontSize: 11 }}
                            tickFormatter={(val) => new Date(val).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' })}
                        />
                        <YAxis
                            tick={{ fontSize: 11 }}
                            tickFormatter={(val) => `${(val / 1000).toFixed(0)}k`}
                        />
                        <Tooltip
                            formatter={(value, name) => [formatCurrency(value), name === 'actual' ? 'Actual' : 'Forecast']}
                            labelFormatter={(label) => new Date(label).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' })}
                        />
                        <Area
                            type="monotone"
                            dataKey="actual"
                            stroke="#3B82F6"
                            fill="url(#actualGradient)"
                            strokeWidth={2}
                            name="Actual"
                        />
                        <Area
                            type="monotone"
                            dataKey="predicted"
                            stroke="#10B981"
                            fill="url(#forecastGradient)"
                            strokeWidth={2}
                            strokeDasharray="5 5"
                            name="Forecast"
                        />
                        <Area
                            type="monotone"
                            dataKey="upper"
                            stroke="transparent"
                            fill="#10B981"
                            fillOpacity={0.1}
                        />
                        <Area
                            type="monotone"
                            dataKey="lower"
                            stroke="transparent"
                            fill="#FFFFFF"
                        />
                        <ReferenceLine
                            x={statsByDate[statsByDate.length - 1]?.date}
                            stroke="#6B7280"
                            strokeDasharray="3 3"
                            label={{ value: 'Today', position: 'top', fontSize: 11 }}
                        />
                    </AreaChart>
                </ResponsiveContainer>
            </div>

            {/* Weekly Pattern */}
            {predictions.insights?.seasonalPattern && (
                <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4">
                    <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Weekly Revenue Pattern</h4>
                    <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={200}>
                        <BarChart data={predictions.insights.seasonalPattern.map((factor, i) => ({
                            day: ['Sun', 'Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat'][i],
                            factor: ((factor - 1) * 100).toFixed(1),
                            isPositive: factor >= 1
                        }))}>
                            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#E5E7EB" />
                            <XAxis dataKey="day" tick={{ fontSize: 12 }} />
                            <YAxis
                                tick={{ fontSize: 11 }}
                                tickFormatter={(val) => `${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}%`}
                            />
                            <Tooltip formatter={(val) => [`${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}%`, 'vs Average']} />
                            <Bar dataKey="factor">
                                {predictions.insights.seasonalPattern.map((factor, index) => (
                                    <Cell
                                        key={index}
                                        fill={factor >= 1 ? '#10B981' : '#EF4444'}
                                    />
                                ))}
                            </Bar>
                            <ReferenceLine y={0} stroke="#6B7280" />
                        </BarChart>
                    </ResponsiveContainer>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-2 text-center">
                        Revenue deviation from weekly average by day of week
                    </p>
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// ANOMALIES TAB
// ============================================================================

const AnomaliesTab = ({ analytics, statsByDate, hasFinancialAccess, formatCurrency, formatNumber }) => {
    const { anomalies } = analytics;

    const carAnomalies = anomalies.cars.filter(a => a.isAnomaly);
    const dailyAnomalies = anomalies.daily.filter(a => a.isAnomaly);

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Summary */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <ArrowUpRight className="w-5 h-5 text-green-600" />
                        <span className="font-medium text-green-800">High Performers</span>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-green-900 mt-2">
                        {carAnomalies.filter(a => a.anomalyType === 'high').length}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-green-600">Cars exceeding expectations</p>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <ArrowDownRight className="w-5 h-5 text-red-600" />
                        <span className="font-medium text-red-800">Underperformers</span>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-red-900 mt-2">
                        {carAnomalies.filter(a => a.anomalyType === 'low').length}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-red-600">Cars needing attention</p>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <Calendar className="w-5 h-5 text-amber-600" />
                        <span className="font-medium text-amber-800">Unusual Days</span>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-amber-900 mt-2">
                        {dailyAnomalies.length}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">Days with anomalous revenue</p>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Car Anomalies Table */}
            {carAnomalies.length > 0 && (
                <div>
                    <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">Car Performance Anomalies</h4>
                    <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                        <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
                            <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                                <tr>
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Status</th>
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Car</th>
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Company</th>
                                    {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">EGP/km</th>
                                    )}
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Score</th>
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Severity</th>
                                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Recommendation</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                                {carAnomalies.sort((a, b) => b.severity - a.severity).map((anomaly, index) => (
                                    <tr key={index} className={anomaly.anomalyType === 'high' ? 'bg-green-50' : 'bg-red-50'}>
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3">
                                            {anomaly.anomalyType === 'high' ? (
                                                <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-green-100 text-green-800">
                                                    <ArrowUpRight className="w-3 h-3" /> High
                                                </span>
                                            ) : (
                                                <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-red-100 text-red-800">
                                                    <ArrowDownRight className="w-3 h-3" /> Low
                                                </span>
                                            )}
                                        </td>
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{anomaly.car}</td>
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700">{anomaly.company}</td>
                                        {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">
                                                {formatNumber(anomaly.value)}
                                            </td>
                                        )}
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">{anomaly.score}/100</td>
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                                            <span className={`text-sm font-medium ${anomaly.severity > 2 ? 'text-red-600' :
                                                    anomaly.severity > 1 ? 'text-amber-600' : 'text-gray-600'
                                                }`}>
                                                {anomaly.severity.toFixed(1)}σ
                                            </span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-600">
                                            {anomaly.anomalyType === 'high'
                                                ? 'Study routes & practices for replication'
                                                : 'Check maintenance, consider route reassignment'}
                                        </td>
                                    </tr>
                                ))}
                            </tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}

            {/* Daily Anomalies */}
            {dailyAnomalies.length > 0 && hasFinancialAccess && (
                <div>
                    <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">Daily Revenue Anomalies</h4>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-3">
                        {dailyAnomalies.map((anomaly, index) => (
                            <div
                                key={index}
                                className={`rounded-lg p-3 border ${anomaly.anomalyType === 'high'
                                        ? 'bg-green-50 border-green-200'
                                        : 'bg-red-50 border-red-200'
                                    }`}
                            >
                                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                                    <div>
                                        <p className="font-medium text-gray-900">
                                            {new Date(anomaly.date).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                                                weekday: 'short',
                                                month: 'short',
                                                day: 'numeric'
                                            })}
                                        </p>
                                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
                                            {formatCurrency(anomaly.value)}
                                        </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <span className={`text-sm font-bold ${anomaly.anomalyType === 'high' ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600'
                                        }`}>
                                        {anomaly.anomalyType === 'high' ? '+' : ''}{anomaly.severity.toFixed(1)}σ
                                    </span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        ))}
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}

            {carAnomalies.length === 0 && dailyAnomalies.length === 0 && (
                <div className="text-center py-12 text-gray-500">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-4 text-green-500" />
                    <p className="font-medium">All metrics within normal range</p>
                    <p className="text-sm">No significant anomalies detected in the current period</p>
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// CAR PERFORMANCE TAB
// ============================================================================

const CarPerformanceTab = ({
    analytics,
    hasFinancialAccess,
    formatCurrency,
    formatNumber,
    selectedCar,
    setSelectedCar
}) => {
    const { carPerformance } = analytics;

    // Sort by score
    const sortedCars = [...carPerformance].sort((a, b) => b.totalScore - a.totalScore);

    // Grade distribution
    const gradeDistribution = sortedCars.reduce((acc, car) => {
        acc[car.grade] = (acc[car.grade] || 0) + 1;
        return acc;
    }, {});

    const getGradeColor = (grade) => {
        switch (grade) {
            case 'A': return 'bg-green-500';
            case 'B': return 'bg-blue-500';
            case 'C': return 'bg-amber-500';
            case 'D': return 'bg-red-500';
            default: return 'bg-gray-500';
        }
    };

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Grade Distribution */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                {['A', 'B', 'C', 'D'].map(grade => (
                    <div key={grade} className="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-4 text-center">
                        <div className={`inline-flex items-center justify-center w-10 h-10 rounded-full text-white font-bold mb-2 ${getGradeColor(grade)}`}>
                            {grade}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">{gradeDistribution[grade] || 0}</p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
                            {grade === 'A' ? 'Excellent' : grade === 'B' ? 'Good' : grade === 'C' ? 'Fair' : 'Needs Work'}
                        </p>
                    </div>
                ))}
            </div>

            {/* Performance Scatter Plot */}
            {hasFinancialAccess && (
                <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4">
                    <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Performance Matrix (Revenue vs Utilization)</h4>
                    <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={300}>
                        <ScatterChart margin={{ top: 20, right: 20, bottom: 20, left: 20 }}>
                            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
                            <XAxis
                                type="number"
                                dataKey="utilization"
                                name="Utilization"
                                tick={{ fontSize: 11 }}
                                label={{ value: 'Utilization %', position: 'bottom', offset: 0 }}
                            />
                            <YAxis
                                type="number"
                                dataKey="revenuePerKm"
                                name="Revenue/km"
                                tick={{ fontSize: 11 }}
                                label={{ value: 'EGP/km', angle: -90, position: 'insideLeft' }}
                            />
                            <ZAxis type="number" dataKey="totalScore" range={[50, 200]} />
                            <Tooltip
                                content={({ payload }) => {
                                    if (!payload?.[0]) return null;
                                    const data = payload[0].payload;
                                    return (
                                        <div className="bg-white p-3 border rounded-lg shadow-lg">
                                            <p className="font-bold">{data.car}</p>
                                            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{data.company}</p>
                                            <p className="text-sm">Score: {data.totalScore}/100 ({data.grade})</p>
                                            <p className="text-sm">Utilization: {data.utilization?.toFixed(0)}%</p>
                                            <p className="text-sm">EGP/km: {formatNumber(data.revenuePerKm)}</p>
                                        </div>
                                    );
                                }}
                            />
                            <Scatter
                                data={sortedCars.map(c => ({
                                    ...c,
                                    utilization: c.scores?.utilization || 0,
                                    revenuePerKm: c.metrics?.revenuePerKm || 0
                                }))}
                            >
                                {sortedCars.map((car, index) => (
                                    <Cell
                                        key={index}
                                        fill={getGradeColor(car.grade).replace('bg-', '#').replace('-500', '')}
                                        cursor="pointer"
                                        onClick={() => setSelectedCar(car)}
                                    />
                                ))}
                            </Scatter>
                        </ScatterChart>
                    </ResponsiveContainer>
                </div>
            )}

            {/* Car Performance Table */}
            <div>
                <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">All Cars Performance</h4>
                <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                    <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
                        <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                            <tr>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Car</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Company</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Grade</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Score</th>
                                {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                    <>
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">EGP/km</th>
                                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">EGP/L</th>
                                    </>
                                )}
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Utilization</th>
                                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">Trips/Day</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                            {sortedCars.map((car, index) => (
                                <tr
                                    key={index}
                                    className={`hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer ${selectedCar?.car === car.car ? 'bg-blue-50' : ''}`}
                                    onClick={() => setSelectedCar(car)}
                                >
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{car.car}</td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700">{car.company}</td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-center">
                                        <span className={`inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-full text-white font-bold text-sm ${getGradeColor(car.grade)}`}>
                                            {car.grade}
                                        </span>
                                    </td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 text-right">{car.totalScore}</td>
                                    {hasFinancialAccess && (
                                        <>
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">
                                                {formatNumber(car.metrics?.revenuePerKm || 0)}
                                            </td>
                                            <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">
                                                {formatNumber(car.metrics?.revenuePerLiter || 0)}
                                            </td>
                                        </>
                                    )}
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">
                                        {(car.metrics?.utilizationRate * 100)?.toFixed(0) || 0}%
                                    </td>
                                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-700 text-right">
                                        {car.metrics?.tripsPerDay?.toFixed(1) || 0}
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                            ))}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Selected Car Detail */}
            {selectedCar && (
                <div className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                        <div>
                            <h4 className="font-bold text-gray-900">{selectedCar.car} Detail</h4>
                            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{selectedCar.company}</p>
                        </div>
                        <button
                            onClick={() => setSelectedCar(null)}
                            className="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600"
                        >
                            ×
                        </button>
                    </div>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Overall Score</p>
                            <p className="text-lg font-bold">{selectedCar.totalScore}/100 ({selectedCar.grade})</p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Revenue/km Score</p>
                            <p className="text-lg font-bold">{selectedCar.scores?.revenuePerKm?.toFixed(0) || 0}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Utilization Score</p>
                            <p className="text-lg font-bold">{selectedCar.scores?.utilization?.toFixed(0) || 0}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Productivity Score</p>
                            <p className="text-lg font-bold">{selectedCar.scores?.productivity?.toFixed(0) || 0}</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
};

// ============================================================================
// OPTIMIZATION TAB
// ============================================================================

const OptimizationTab = ({ analytics, formatCurrency, formatNumber }) => {
    const { suggestions, optimizationPotential, companyMetrics } = analytics;

    const getPriorityColor = (priority) => {
        switch (priority) {
            case 'high': return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800 border-red-200';
            case 'medium': return 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-800 border-amber-200';
            case 'low': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 border-blue-200';
            default: return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800 border-gray-200';
        }
    };

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Optimization Potential */}
            <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-green-50 to-emerald-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-6">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
                    <div className="bg-green-100 p-2 rounded-full">
                        <Zap className="w-6 h-6 text-green-600" />
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <h3 className="font-bold text-gray-900">Optimization Potential</h3>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">If all cars performed at top 20% level</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                    <div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Current Revenue</p>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                            {formatCurrency(optimizationPotential.currentRevenue)}
                        </p>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Potential Revenue</p>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600">
                            {formatCurrency(optimizationPotential.potentialRevenue)}
                        </p>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Improvement</p>
                        <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600">
                            +{formatCurrency(optimizationPotential.improvementAmount)}
                            <span className="text-sm font-normal text-gray-600 ml-1">
                                ({optimizationPotential.improvementPercent.toFixed(1)}%)
                            </span>
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* Reallocation Suggestions */}
            {suggestions.length > 0 && (
                <div>
                    <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">Recommended Actions</h4>
                    <div className="space-y-3">
                        {suggestions.map((suggestion, index) => (
                            <div
                                key={index}
                                className={`border rounded-lg p-4 ${getPriorityColor(suggestion.priority)}`}
                            >
                                <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                                    {suggestion.type === 'reallocation' ? (
                                        <Shuffle className="w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
                                    ) : (
                                        <Target className="w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
                                    )}
                                    <div className="flex-1">
                                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                                            <span className={`text-xs font-medium px-2 py-0.5 rounded uppercase`}>
                                                {suggestion.priority} priority
                                            </span>
                                            {suggestion.type === 'reallocation' && (
                                                <span className="text-xs bg-white/50 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">
                                                    Car Reallocation
                                                </span>
                                            )}
                                        </div>

                                        {suggestion.type === 'reallocation' ? (
                                            <>
                                                <p className="font-medium text-gray-900">
                                                    Move {suggestion.car} from {suggestion.fromCompany} to {suggestion.toCompany}
                                                </p>
                                                <p className="text-sm mt-1">{suggestion.reason}</p>
                                                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mt-2 text-sm">
                                                    <span>Current Score: {suggestion.currentScore}/100</span>
                                                    <span className="text-green-700 font-medium">
                                                        Expected Improvement: +{suggestion.expectedImprovement}%
                                                    </span>
                                                    {suggestion.potentialGain > 0 && (
                                                        <span className="text-green-700 font-medium">
                                                            Potential Gain: {formatCurrency(suggestion.potentialGain)}
                                                        </span>
                                                    )}
                                                </div>
                                            </>
                                        ) : (
                                            <>
                                                <p className="font-medium text-gray-900">{suggestion.recommendation}</p>
                                                <p className="text-sm mt-1">{suggestion.reason}</p>
                                            </>
                                        )}
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        ))}
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}

            {/* Company Profitability Ranking */}
            <div>
                <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">Company Profitability Ranking</h4>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4">
                    Consider shifting capacity towards higher-ranked companies when possible
                </p>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                    {[...companyMetrics]
                        .sort((a, b) => b.revenuePerKm - a.revenuePerKm)
                        .map((company, index) => (
                            <div
                                key={company.company}
                                className={`flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg ${index === 0 ? 'bg-green-50 border border-green-200' : 'bg-gray-50'
                                    }`}
                            >
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                                    <span className={`w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-sm ${index === 0 ? 'bg-green-500 text-white' : 'bg-gray-300 text-gray-700'
                                        }`}>
                                        {index + 1}
                                    </span>
                                    <span className="font-medium text-gray-900">{company.company}</span>
                                </div>
                                <div className="text-right">
                                    <p className="font-bold text-gray-900">{formatNumber(company.revenuePerKm)} EGP/km</p>
                                    <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{formatNumber(company.revenuePerLiter)} EGP/L</p>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        ))}
                </div>
            </div>

            {suggestions.length === 0 && (
                <div className="text-center py-12 text-gray-500">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-4 text-green-500" />
                    <p className="font-medium">Fleet is well optimized</p>
                    <p className="text-sm">No significant reallocation opportunities detected</p>
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
};

export default TripAnalyticsInsights;
===== ./TripList.jsx =====
import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
import apiClient from '../../apiClient';

// Import existing trip components
import SearchBar from './SearchBar';
import FilterPanel from './FilterPanel';
import ActiveFilters from './ActiveFilters';
import DeleteConfirmationModal from './DeleteConfirmationModal';
import ParentTripDeleteModal from './ParentTripDeleteModal';
import TripTable from './TripTable.tsx';
import Pagination from './Pagination';
import ListActions from './ListActions';
import NoResultsAlert from './NoResultsAlert';
import LocationDialog from '../LocationDialog';
import ReceiptDialog from './ReceiptDialog';

// Import icons
import { List, BarChart3 } from 'lucide-react';
import TripStatistics from './TripStatistics';

const TripList = () => {
  // Function to get the first day of current month
  const getFirstDayOfMonth = () => {
    const now = new Date();
    const year = now.getFullYear();
    const month = now.getMonth();
    const firstDay = new Date(year, month, 1);
    return firstDay.toLocaleDateString('en-CA');
  };

  // Function to get today's date
  const getToday = () => {
    return new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  };

  // Separate limit state from meta
  const [limit, setLimit] = useState(10);
  const [meta, setMeta] = useState({
    page: 1,
    pages: 1,
    total: 0,
  });

  const [showReceiptDialog, setShowReceiptDialog] = useState(false);
  const [selectedTripForReceipt, setSelectedTripForReceipt] = useState(null);
  const [shouldRefresh, setShouldRefresh] = useState(false);

  // State for tab management
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('list');

  // State declarations for trip list
  const [trips, setTrips] = useState([]);
  const [companies, setCompanies] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(1);
  const [sortConfig, setSortConfig] = useState({
    key: null,
    direction: 'ascending'
  });
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState({
    company: '',
    startDate: getFirstDayOfMonth(),
    endDate: getToday(),
    missingData: '',
    receiptStatus: ''
  });
  
  // Global search state
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
  const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
  
  // Delete confirmation modal state for single trips
  const [showDeleteModal, setShowDeleteModal] = useState(false);
  const [tripToDelete, setTripToDelete] = useState(null);
  const [isDeleting, setIsDeleting] = useState(false);

  // Delete confirmation modal state for parent trips
  const [showDeleteParentModal, setShowDeleteParentModal] = useState(false);
  const [parentToDelete, setParentToDelete] = useState(null);
  const [parentContainerCount, setParentContainerCount] = useState(0);
  const [isDeletingParent, setIsDeletingParent] = useState(false);

  // Location dialog state
  const [showLocationDialog, setShowLocationDialog] = useState(false);
  const [locationData, setLocationData] = useState({
    dropOffLocation: null,
    terminalLocation: null,
    routeData: null
  });
  const [selectedTripDetails, setSelectedTripDetails] = useState({});
  const [isLoadingDetails, setIsLoadingDetails] = useState(false);

  // Memoized callbacks
  const handleOpenReceiptDialog = useCallback((tripId) => {
    setSelectedTripForReceipt(tripId);
    setShowReceiptDialog(true);
  }, []);

  const handleCloseReceiptDialog = useCallback(() => {
    setShowReceiptDialog(false);
    setSelectedTripForReceipt(null);
    setShouldRefresh(prev => !prev);
  }, []);

  const fetchCompanies = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.get(`/api/mappings/companies`);
      setCompanies(response.data.data || []);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch companies:', err);
    }
  }, []);

  const fetchTrips = useCallback(async (pageNumber = currentPage, pageLimit = limit) => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    setError('');
    
    try {
      let url = `/api/trips`;
      let params = {
        page: pageNumber,
        limit: pageLimit
      };
      
      if (searchTerm) {
        params.search = searchTerm;
      }
      
      if (filters.missingData) {
        params.missing_data = filters.missingData;
      }
      
      if (filters.receiptStatus) {
        params.receipt_status = filters.receiptStatus;
      }
      
      if (filters.company) {
        url = `/api/trips/company/${filters.company}`;
      }
      
      if (filters.startDate && filters.endDate) {
        url = `/api/trips/date`;
        params = {
          ...params,
          start_date: filters.startDate,
          end_date: filters.endDate
        };
        
        if (filters.company) {
          params.company = filters.company;
        }
      }
      
      const response = await apiClient.get(url, { params });
      setTrips(response.data.data || []);
      
      if (response.data.meta) {
        setMeta({
          page: response.data.meta.page,
          pages: response.data.meta.pages,
          total: response.data.meta.total,
        });
        setTotalPages(response.data.meta.pages || 1);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Failed to fetch trips: ' + (err.response?.data?.message || err.message));
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
      setIsSearching(false);
    }
  }, [currentPage, limit, searchTerm, filters.missingData, filters.receiptStatus, filters.company, filters.startDate, filters.endDate]);

  // Initial fetch of companies
  useEffect(() => {
    fetchCompanies();
  }, [fetchCompanies]);

  // Fetch trips when dependencies change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeTab === 'list') {
      fetchTrips();
    }
  }, [
    fetchTrips,
    activeTab,
    shouldRefresh
  ]);

  const fetchAllTrips = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsExporting(true);
    try {
      let url = `/api/trips`;
      let params = { limit: 10000 };
      
      if (searchTerm) {
        params.search = searchTerm;
      }

      if (filters.missingData) {
        params.missing_data = filters.missingData;
      }
      
      if (filters.receiptStatus) {
        params.receipt_status = filters.receiptStatus;
      }
      
      if (filters.company) {
        url = `/api/trips/company/${filters.company}`;
      }
      
      if (filters.startDate && filters.endDate) {
        url = `/api/trips/date`;
        params = {
          ...params,
          start_date: filters.startDate,
          end_date: filters.endDate
        };
        
        if (filters.company) {
          params.company = filters.company;
        }
      }
      
      const response = await apiClient.get(url, { params });
      return response.data.data || [];
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Failed to export trips: ' + (err.response?.data?.message || err.message));
      console.error(err);
      return [];
    } finally {
      setIsExporting(false);
    }
  }, [searchTerm, filters]);

  const handleLimitChange = useCallback((newLimit) => {
    setLimit(newLimit);
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleShowDetails = useCallback(async (tripId) => {
    setIsLoadingDetails(true);
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.get(`/api/trips/${tripId}/details`);
      
      if (response.data && 
          response.data.drop_off_point_location && 
          response.data.terminal_location &&
          response.data.drop_off_point_location.lat && 
          response.data.drop_off_point_location.lng &&
          response.data.terminal_location.lat && 
          response.data.terminal_location.lng) {
        
        setLocationData({
          dropOffLocation: response.data.drop_off_point_location,
          terminalLocation: response.data.terminal_location,
          routeData: response.data.route_data || null
        });
        
        setSelectedTripDetails({
          company: response.data.data.company,
          terminal: response.data.data.terminal,
          drop_off_point: response.data.data.drop_off_point,
          receipt_no: response.data.data.receipt_no,
          mileage: response.data.data.mileage || response.data.data.distance,
          revenue: response.data.data.revenue || response.data.data.fee,
          car_id: response.data.data.car_id,
          date: response.data.data.date,
          id: response.data.data.ID,
        });
        
        setShowLocationDialog(true);
      } else {
        setError('No location data available for this trip.');
        setTimeout(() => setError(''), 5000);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching trip details:', error);
      setError('Failed to fetch trip details: ' + (error.response?.data?.message || error.message));
      setTimeout(() => setError(''), 5000);
    } finally {
      setIsLoadingDetails(false);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleFilterChange = useCallback((e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleClearReceiptStatus = useCallback(() => {
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, receiptStatus: '' }));
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleResetFilters = useCallback(() => {
    setFilters({
      company: '',
      startDate: '',
      endDate: '',
      missingData: '',
      receiptStatus: ''
    });
    setSearchTerm('');
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleClearMissingData = useCallback(() => {
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, missingData: '' }));
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleSearchChange = useCallback((e) => {
    setSearchTerm(e.target.value);
  }, []);

  const handleSearch = useCallback(() => {
    setIsSearching(true);
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const handleSearchKeyPress = useCallback((e) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
      handleSearch();
    }
  }, [handleSearch]);

  const handlePageChange = useCallback((page) => {
    setCurrentPage(page);
  }, []);
  
  
  // Delete handlers
  const openDeleteModal = useCallback((id) => {
    setTripToDelete(id);
    setShowDeleteModal(true);
  }, []);

  const closeDeleteModal = useCallback(() => {
    setShowDeleteModal(false);
    setTimeout(() => setTripToDelete(null), 200);
  }, []);

  const handleDelete = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!tripToDelete) return;
    
    setIsDeleting(true);
    try {
      await apiClient.delete(`/api/trips/${tripToDelete}`);
      fetchTrips();
      closeDeleteModal();
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Failed to delete trip: ' + (err.response?.data?.message || err.message));
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setIsDeleting(false);
    }
  }, [tripToDelete, fetchTrips, closeDeleteModal]);

  const openDeleteParentModal = useCallback((parentId) => {
    const parentContainers = trips.filter(t => t.parent_trip_id === parentId);
    setParentToDelete(parentId);
    setParentContainerCount(parentContainers.length);
    setShowDeleteParentModal(true);
  }, [trips]);

  const closeDeleteParentModal = useCallback(() => {
    setShowDeleteParentModal(false);
    setTimeout(() => {
      setParentToDelete(null);
      setParentContainerCount(0);
    }, 200);
  }, []);

  const handleDeleteParent = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!parentToDelete) return;
    
    setIsDeletingParent(true);
    try {
      await apiClient.delete(`/api/trips/parent/${parentToDelete}`);
      fetchTrips();
      closeDeleteParentModal();
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Failed to delete parent trip: ' + (err.response?.data?.message || err.message));
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setIsDeletingParent(false);
    }
  }, [parentToDelete, fetchTrips, closeDeleteParentModal]);
  
  const requestSort = useCallback((key) => {
    setSortConfig(prev => ({
      key,
      direction: prev.key === key && prev.direction === 'ascending' ? 'descending' : 'ascending'
    }));
  }, []);
  
  // Client-side sorting only (backend handles filtering)
  const sortedTrips = useMemo(() => {
    if (!sortConfig.key) return trips;
    
    const sortableItems = [...trips];
    sortableItems.sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortConfig.key];
      let bValue = b[sortConfig.key];
      
      if (typeof aValue === 'number' && typeof bValue === 'number') {
        return sortConfig.direction === 'ascending' ? aValue - bValue : bValue - aValue;
      }
      
      if (sortConfig.key === 'date') {
        return sortConfig.direction === 'ascending' 
          ? new Date(aValue) - new Date(bValue) 
          : new Date(bValue) - new Date(aValue);
      }
      
      if (aValue && bValue) {
        aValue = aValue.toString().toLowerCase();
        bValue = bValue.toString().toLowerCase();
        return sortConfig.direction === 'ascending'
          ? aValue.localeCompare(bValue)
          : bValue.localeCompare(aValue);
      }
      
      if (aValue === null || aValue === undefined) return sortConfig.direction === 'ascending' ? -1 : 1;
      if (bValue === null || bValue === undefined) return sortConfig.direction === 'ascending' ? 1 : -1;
      
      return 0;
    });
    return sortableItems;
  }, [trips, sortConfig]);

  const hasActiveFilters = searchTerm || filters.company || filters.startDate || filters.endDate || filters.missingData || filters.receiptStatus;

  return (
    <div className="w-full overflow-auto px-2 sm:px-4 md:px-6 py-2 sm:py-4">
      {showDeleteModal && (
        <DeleteConfirmationModal
          isDeleting={isDeleting}
          onClose={closeDeleteModal}
          onDelete={handleDelete}
        />
      )}

      {showDeleteParentModal && (
        <ParentTripDeleteModal
          isDeleting={isDeletingParent}
          containerCount={parentContainerCount}
          onClose={closeDeleteParentModal}
          onDelete={handleDeleteParent}
        />
      )}

      <ReceiptDialog
        isOpen={showReceiptDialog}
        onClose={handleCloseReceiptDialog}
        tripId={selectedTripForReceipt}
        apiClient={apiClient}
      />

      <LocationDialog
        isOpen={showLocationDialog}
        onClose={() => setShowLocationDialog(false)}
        dropOffLocation={locationData.dropOffLocation}
        terminalLocation={locationData.terminalLocation}
        isEdit={false}
        tripDetails={selectedTripDetails}
        routeData={locationData.routeData}
      />

      {isLoadingDetails && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 flex flex-col items-center">
            <svg className="animate-spin h-8 w-8 text-blue-600 mb-3" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <circle className="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="4"></circle>
              <path className="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path>
            </svg>
            <p className="text-gray-600">Loading trip details...</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="bg-white shadow-md rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
        <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-blue-800 px-3 sm:px-4 py-3 sm:py-4">
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
            <h2 className="text-lg sm:text-xl font-bold text-white">Trip Management</h2>
            
            <div className="flex bg-blue-700 rounded-md">
              <button
                className={`flex items-center px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium rounded-md transition-colors ${
                  activeTab === 'list' 
                    ? 'bg-white text-blue-700' 
                    : 'text-white hover:bg-blue-600'
                }`}
                onClick={() => setActiveTab('list')}
              >
                <List size={16} className="mr-1.5" />
                Trip List
              </button>
              <button
                className={`flex items-center px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium rounded-md transition-colors ${
                  activeTab === 'statistics' 
                    ? 'bg-white text-blue-700' 
                    : 'text-white hover:bg-blue-600'
                }`}
                onClick={() => setActiveTab('statistics')}
              >
                <BarChart3 size={16} className="mr-1.5" />
                Statistics
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-3 sm:p-4 md:p-6 space-y-4">
          {error && (
            <div className="bg-red-100 border-l-4 border-red-500 text-red-700 p-3 sm:p-4 rounded" role="alert">
              <p className="font-medium">Error</p>
              <p className="text-sm">{error}</p>
            </div>
          )}
          
          <FilterPanel
            companies={companies}
            filters={filters}
            onChange={handleFilterChange}
            onReset={handleResetFilters}
          />

          {activeTab === 'list' ? (
            <>
              <SearchBar
                searchTerm={searchTerm}
                isSearching={isSearching}
                onChange={handleSearchChange}
                onSearch={handleSearch}
                onKeyPress={handleSearchKeyPress}
                onClear={() => setSearchTerm('')}
              />
              
              <ActiveFilters
                searchTerm={searchTerm}
                filters={filters}
                onClearSearch={() => setSearchTerm('')}
                onClearCompany={() => setFilters({...filters, company: ''})}
                onClearDates={() => setFilters({...filters, startDate: '', endDate: ''})}
                onClearMissingData={handleClearMissingData}
                onClearReceiptStatus={handleClearReceiptStatus}
              />
              
              <ListActions
                isLoading={isLoading}
                isExporting={isExporting}
                tripsCount={sortedTrips.length}
                onExport={fetchAllTrips}
              />
              
              {hasActiveFilters && sortedTrips.length === 0 && !isLoading && (
                <NoResultsAlert />
              )}
              
              {isLoading && (
                <div className="flex justify-center p-8">
                  <div className="w-12 h-12 border-4 border-blue-600 border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin"></div>
                </div>
              )}
              
              {!isLoading && (
  <TripTable
    isLoading={isLoading}
    trips={sortedTrips}
    sortConfig={sortConfig}
    onSort={requestSort}
    onDelete={openDeleteModal}
    onDeleteParent={openDeleteParentModal}
    onShowDetails={handleShowDetails}
    onManageReceipt={handleOpenReceiptDialog}
  />
)}
              
       
              
              {totalPages > 1 && (
                <Pagination
                  currentPage={currentPage}
                  totalPages={totalPages}
                  total={meta.total}
                  limit={limit}
                  onPageChange={handlePageChange}
                  onLimitChange={handleLimitChange}
                  isLoading={isLoading}
                />
              )}
            </>
          ) : (
            <TripStatistics filters={filters} />
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default TripList;
===== ./TripReportGarage.jsx =====
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import apiClient from '../../apiClient';
import { Printer, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';

const TripReportGarage = () => {
  const getYesterday = () => {
    const yesterday = new Date();
    yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
    return yesterday.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  };

  const [trips, setTrips] = useState([]);
  const [companies, setCompanies] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState({
    startDate: getYesterday(),
    endDate: getYesterday(),
    company: 'watanya'
  });
  const [submittedStatus, setSubmittedStatus] = useState({});
  const [customRows, setCustomRows] = useState([]);
  const [nextCustomId, setNextCustomId] = useState(-1);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchCompanies();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (filters.company && filters.startDate && filters.endDate) {
      fetchTrips();
    }
  }, [filters]);

  const fetchCompanies = async () => {
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.get('/api/mappings/companies');
      setCompanies(response.data.data || []);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch companies:', err);
    }
  };

  const fetchTrips = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    setError('');

    try {
      const response = await apiClient.get('/api/trips/date', {
        params: {
          start_date: filters.startDate,
          end_date: filters.endDate,
          company: filters.company,
          page: 1,
          limit: 1000
        }
      });
      
      const fetchedTrips = response.data.data || [];
      setTrips(fetchedTrips);

      const initialStatus = {};
      fetchedTrips.forEach(trip => {
        initialStatus[trip.ID] = false;
      });
      setSubmittedStatus(prev => ({ ...prev, ...initialStatus }));
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.message || err.message);
      setTrips([]);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const handleFilterChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
  };

  const handleSubmittedToggle = (tripId) => {
    setSubmittedStatus(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      [tripId]: !prev[tripId]
    }));
  };

  const handleAddRow = () => {
    const newRow = {
      ID: nextCustomId,
      receipt_no: '',
      driver_name: '',
      date: filters.startDate,
      car_no_plate: '',
      tank_capacity: '',
      isCustom: true
    };
    setCustomRows(prev => [...prev, newRow]);
    setSubmittedStatus(prev => ({ ...prev, [nextCustomId]: false }));
    setNextCustomId(prev => prev - 1);
  };

  const handleRemoveRow = (tripId) => {
    if (tripId < 0) {
      setCustomRows(prev => prev.filter(row => row.ID !== tripId));
    } else {
      setTrips(prev => prev.filter(trip => trip.ID !== tripId));
    }
    setSubmittedStatus(prev => {
      const newStatus = { ...prev };
      delete newStatus[tripId];
      return newStatus;
    });
  };

  const handleCustomRowChange = (tripId, field, value) => {
    setCustomRows(prev => prev.map(row => 
      row.ID === tripId ? { ...row, [field]: value } : row
    ));
  };

  const formatDateArabic = (dateString) => {
    if (!dateString) return 'غير متوفر';
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('ar-EG', { 
      year: 'numeric', 
      month: 'long', 
      day: 'numeric' 
    });
  };

  const formatDateEnglish = (dateString) => {
    if (!dateString) return 'N/A';
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
      year: 'numeric', 
      month: 'short', 
      day: 'numeric' 
    });
  };

  const handlePrint = () => {
    const allRows = [...trips, ...customRows];
    const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
    const companyName = filters.company.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + filters.company.slice(1);
    
    const printContent = `
      <!DOCTYPE html>
      <html dir="rtl" lang="ar">
      <head>
        <meta charset="UTF-8">
        <title>تقرير رحلات ${companyName}</title>
        <style>
          @page { size: A4; margin: 15mm; }
          body { font-family: 'Cairo', 'Arial', sans-serif; direction: rtl; padding: 15px; }
          .header { text-align: center; margin-bottom: 25px; border-bottom: 2px solid #2563eb; padding-bottom: 12px; }
          .header h1 { color: #1e40af; font-size: 22px; margin: 0; }
          table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; margin-top: 15px; }
          th, td { border: 1px solid #cbd5e1; padding: 8px; text-align: right; font-size: 14px; }
          th { background-color: #f1f5f9; color: #1e40af; font-weight: bold; }
          tr:nth-child(even) { background-color: #f9fafb; }
          .checkbox-cell { text-align: center; }
          .checkbox { width: 16px; height: 16px; }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="header">
          <h1>تقرير رحلات شركة ${companyName}</h1>
        </div>
        <table>
          <thead>
            <tr>
              <th>رقم الإيصال</th>
              <th>اسم السائق</th>
              <th>التاريخ</th>
              <th>رقم اللوحة</th>
              <th>سعة الخزان</th>
              <th class="checkbox-cell">تم التسليم</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            ${allRows.map(trip => `
              <tr>
                <td>${trip.receipt_no || 'غير متوفر'}</td>
                <td>${trip.driver_name || 'غير متوفر'}</td>
                <td>${formatDateArabic(trip.date)}</td>
                <td>${trip.car_no_plate || 'غير متوفر'}</td>
                <td>${trip.tank_capacity || 'غير متوفر'} لتر</td>
                <td class="checkbox-cell">
                  <input type="checkbox" class="checkbox" ${submittedStatus[trip.ID] ? 'checked' : ''} />
                </td>
              </tr>
            `).join('')}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </body>
      </html>
    `;
    
    printWindow.document.write(printContent);
    printWindow.document.close();
    printWindow.focus();
