                </div>

                {/* Map Controls */}
                <button
                  onClick={() => setSatelliteView(!satelliteView)}
                  className={`flex items-center px-2 sm:px-3 py-1.5 sm:py-2 rounded-lg border transition-all ${
                    satelliteView ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white border-blue-600' : 'bg-white text-gray-700 border-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50'
                  }`}
                  title={satelliteView ? 'Switch to Street View' : 'Switch to Satellite View'}
                >
                  <Layers className="h-3 w-3 sm:h-4 sm:w-4 sm:mr-2" />
                  <span className="hidden sm:inline text-xs">{satelliteView ? 'Street' : 'Satellite'}</span>
                </button>

                <button
                  onClick={handleRecenter}
                  className="p-1.5 sm:p-2 bg-white border border-gray-300 text-gray-700 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors"
                  title="Recenter Map"
                >
                  <Locate className="h-4 w-4" />
                </button>

                <button
                  onClick={toggleFullscreen}
                  className="p-1.5 sm:p-2 bg-white border border-gray-300 text-gray-700 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors"
                  title={isMapFullscreen ? 'Exit Fullscreen' : 'Fullscreen'}
                >
                  {isMapFullscreen ? <Minimize2 className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Maximize2 className="h-4 w-4" />}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Legend */}
            {!isMobile && filteredLegs.length > 0 && (
              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3 sm:gap-4 mt-3 sm:mt-4 pt-3 sm:pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
                {filteredLegs.slice(0, 8).map((leg, index) => {
                  const color = LEG_COLORS[index % LEG_COLORS.length];
                  const isReturnLeg = !leg.trip_struct_id;
                  return (
                    <div 
                      key={leg.id}
                      className={`flex items-center cursor-pointer transition-all ${hoveredLegId === leg.id ? 'scale-110' : ''}`}
                      onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredLegId(leg.id)}
                      onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredLegId(null)}
                      onClick={() => setExpandedLegId(leg.id)}
                    >
                      <div className="w-8 sm:w-12 h-1 rounded mr-2" style={{ backgroundColor: color }}></div>
                      <span className="text-xs font-medium text-gray-700">
                        {isReturnLeg ? '🏁 Return' : `📦 Stop ${leg.sequence_number}`}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
                {(activeRouteView === 'optimal' || activeRouteView === 'both') && (
                  <div className="flex items-center">
                    <div className="w-8 sm:w-12 h-1 bg-green-600 rounded mr-2" style={{ backgroundImage: 'repeating-linear-gradient(90deg, #10b981, #10b981 5px, transparent 5px, transparent 10px)' }}></div>
                    <span className="text-xs font-medium text-gray-700">🛣️ Optimal</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          <div ref={mapRef} className={`bg-gray-100 ${isMapFullscreen ? 'h-[calc(100vh-240px)]' : 'h-[400px] sm:h-[500px] lg:h-[600px]'}`} />

          {/* Playback Controls */}
          {tripData?.location_pings && tripData.location_pings.length > 0 && (
            <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-50 to-gray-100 px-3 sm:px-6 py-3 sm:py-4 border-t border-gray-200">
              <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-4">
                <button
                  onClick={togglePlayPause}
                  className="p-2 sm:p-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors shadow-md hover:shadow-lg flex-shrink-0"
                  title={isPlaying ? 'Pause' : 'Play'}
                >
                  {isPlaying ? <Pause className="h-4 w-4 sm:h-5 sm:w-5" /> : <Play className="h-4 w-4 sm:h-5 sm:w-5" />}
                </button>
                
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <input
                    type="range"
                    min="0"
                    max={tripData.location_pings.length - 1}
                    value={currentPingIndex}
                    onChange={handleSliderChange}
                    className="w-full h-2 bg-gray-200 rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-pointer"
                    style={{
                      background: `linear-gradient(to right, #3b82f6 0%, #3b82f6 ${(currentPingIndex / (tripData.location_pings.length - 1)) * 100}%, #e5e7eb ${(currentPingIndex / (tripData.location_pings.length - 1)) * 100}%, #e5e7eb 100%)`
                    }}
                  />
                </div>

                <div className="hidden sm:flex items-center space-x-2">
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-600">Speed:</span>
                  <select
                    value={playbackSpeed}
                    onChange={(e) => setPlaybackSpeed(parseInt(e.target.value))}
                    className="px-2 py-1 text-xs border border-gray-300 rounded bg-white"
                  >
                    <option value="50">0.5x</option>
                    <option value="100">1x</option>
                    <option value="200">2x</option>
                    <option value="500">5x</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                
                <div className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 min-w-[80px] sm:min-w-[140px] text-right flex-shrink-0">
                  <div className="font-bold">{currentPingIndex + 1} / {tripData.location_pings.length}</div>
                  {tripData.location_pings[currentPingIndex]?.time_stamp && (
                    <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 hidden sm:block">
                      {formatTime(tripData.location_pings[currentPingIndex].time_stamp)}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Performance & Timeline Grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6 sm:gap-8 mb-6 sm:mb-8">
          {/* Performance Metrics */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-xl sm:rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-4 sm:p-6">
            <div className="flex items-center mb-4 sm:mb-6">
              <BarChart3 className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-blue-600 mr-2 sm:mr-3" />
              <h3 className="text-lg sm:text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">Performance Metrics</h3>
            </div>
            
            <div className="space-y-3 sm:space-y-4">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-blue-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-100 transition-colors">
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Distance Deviation</p>
                  <p className="text-xl sm:text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 truncate">{formatDistance(Math.abs(tripData.DistanceDeviation))}</p>
                </div>
                <div className={`px-2 sm:px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ml-2 flex-shrink-0 ${
                  Math.abs(tripData.DistanceDeviation) <= 5 ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 
                  Math.abs(tripData.DistanceDeviation) <= 15 ? 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700' : 
                  'bg-red-100 text-red-700'
                }`}>
                  {tripData.DistanceDeviation > 0 ? '+' : ''}{tripData.DistanceDeviation?.toFixed(1)} km
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-purple-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-purple-100 transition-colors">
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Average Speed</p>
                  <p className="text-xl sm:text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">{tripData.AverageSpeed?.toFixed(1)} km/h</p>
                </div>
                <Gauge className="h-6 w-6 sm:h-8 sm:w-8 text-purple-600 flex-shrink-0" />
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-orange-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-orange-100 transition-colors">
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Time Deviation</p>
                  <p className="text-xl sm:text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 truncate">{formatDuration(Math.abs(tripData.TimeDeviation))}</p>
                </div>
                <div className={`px-2 sm:px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ml-2 flex-shrink-0 ${
                  Math.abs(tripData.TimeDeviation) <= 1800 ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 
                  Math.abs(tripData.TimeDeviation) <= 3600 ? 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700' : 
                  'bg-red-100 text-red-700'
                }`}>
                  {tripData.TimeDeviation > 0 ? '+' : ''}{formatDuration(tripData.TimeDeviation)}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-green-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-green-100 transition-colors">
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Total Deliveries</p>
                  <p className="text-xl sm:text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">{tripData.TotalDeliveries}</p>
                </div>
                <Package className="h-6 w-6 sm:h-8 sm:w-8 text-green-600 flex-shrink-0" />
              </div>

              {tripData.IsComplete ? (
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-green-50 rounded-lg border-2 border-green-200">
                  <div className="flex items-center min-w-0">
                    <CheckCircle className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-green-600 mr-2 sm:mr-3 flex-shrink-0" />
                    <div className="min-w-0">
                      <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-green-700">Trip Complete ✅</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-green-600">All deliveries completed</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 sm:p-4 bg-yellow-50 rounded-lg border-2 border-yellow-200">
                  <div className="flex items-center min-w-0">
                    <AlertCircle className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-yellow-600 mr-2 sm:mr-3 flex-shrink-0" />
                    <div className="min-w-0">
                      <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-yellow-700">Incomplete Trip ⚠️</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-yellow-600">Some deliveries skipped</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Trip Timeline */}
          <div className="bg-white rounded-xl sm:rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-4 sm:p-6">
            <div className="flex items-center mb-4 sm:mb-6">
              <Calendar className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-blue-600 mr-2 sm:mr-3" />
              <h3 className="text-lg sm:text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">Trip Timeline</h3>
            </div>
            
            <div className="space-y-4 sm:space-y-4">
              <div className="flex items-start">
                <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-10 h-10 sm:w-12 sm:h-12 bg-green-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  <Home className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-green-600" />
                </div>
                <div className="ml-3 sm:ml-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">🏁 Trip Started</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 font-mono">{formatTime(tripData.StartTime)}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Departed from terminal</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-start">
                <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-10 h-10 sm:w-12 sm:h-12 bg-blue-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  <Target className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-blue-600" />
                </div>
                <div className="ml-3 sm:ml-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">📦 Deliveries Completed</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 font-mono">{formatTime(tripData.EndTime)}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">{tripData.TotalDeliveries} stops • {formatDuration(tripData.TripDuration)}</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              {tripData.ReturnedToBase && tripData.ReturnTime && (
                <div className="flex items-start">
                  <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-10 h-10 sm:w-12 sm:h-12 bg-green-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                    <CheckCircle className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-green-600" />
                  </div>
                  <div className="ml-3 sm:ml-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">✅ Returned to Base</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 font-mono">{formatTime(tripData.ReturnTime)}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Trip completed successfully</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {!tripData.ReturnedToBase && (
                <div className="flex items-start">
                  <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-10 h-10 sm:w-12 sm:h-12 bg-yellow-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                    <AlertCircle className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-yellow-600" />
                  </div>
                  <div className="ml-3 sm:ml-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">⏳ Return Pending</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-yellow-600">Vehicle has not returned to terminal</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Leg Details */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-xl sm:rounded-2xl shadow-xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-50 to-gray-100 px-3 sm:px-6 py-3 sm:py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3 sm:gap-4">
              <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-4">
                <Route className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6 text-blue-600" />
                <h2 className="text-base sm:text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">Trip Legs</h2>
                <span className="px-2 sm:px-3 py-1 bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 rounded-full text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold">
                  {filteredLegs.length}
                </span>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-3">
                <Filter className="h-4 w-4 sm:h-5 sm:w-5 text-gray-600" />
                <select
                  value={selectedLegFilter}
                  onChange={(e) => setSelectedLegFilter(e.target.value)}
                  className="px-3 sm:px-4 py-1.5 sm:py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500 bg-white text-sm"
                >
                  <option value="all">All ({tripData.ActualLegs?.length || 0})</option>
                  <option value="delivery">Delivery ({deliveryLegs.length})</option>
                  <option value="return">Return ({returnLeg ? 1 : 0})</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="divide-y divide-gray-100">
            {filteredLegs.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="p-8 sm:p-12 text-center">
                <MapPin className="h-12 w-12 sm:h-16 sm:w-16 text-gray-400 mx-auto mb-4" />
                <h3 className="text-base sm:text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-2">No Legs Found</h3>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Try selecting a different filter</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              filteredLegs.map((leg, index) => {
                const isExpanded = expandedLegId === leg.id;
                const containerIds = leg.container_ids ? JSON.parse(leg.container_ids) : (leg.trip_struct_id ? [leg.trip_struct_id] : []);
                const isReturnLeg = !leg.trip_struct_id;
                const color = LEG_COLORS[index % LEG_COLORS.length];

                return (
                  <div 
                    key={leg.id} 
                    className={`${isExpanded ? 'bg-blue-50' : 'hover:bg-gray-50'} transition-all ${hoveredLegId === leg.id ? 'bg-blue-100 shadow-md' : ''}`}
                    onMouseEnter={() => !isMobile && setHoveredLegId(leg.id)}
                    onMouseLeave={() => !isMobile && setHoveredLegId(null)}
                  >
                     <button
                      onClick={() => setExpandedLegId(isExpanded ? null : leg.id)}
                      className="w-full px-3 sm:px-6 py-4 sm:py-5 flex items-center justify-between"
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <div 
                          className={`w-10 h-10 sm:w-12 sm:h-12 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-white shadow-md flex-shrink-0`}
                          style={{ backgroundColor: isReturnLeg ? '#10b981' : color }}
                        >
                          {isReturnLeg ? <Home className="h-5 w-5 sm:h-6 sm:w-6" /> : <span className="text-sm sm:text-base">{leg.sequence_number}</span>}
                        </div>
                        
                        <div className="flex-1 text-left min-w-0">
                          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-3 mb-1">
                            <h4 className="text-sm sm:text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 truncate">
                              {leg.from_name} → {leg.to_name}
                            </h4>
                            {!isReturnLeg && containerIds.length > 0 && (
                              <span className="px-2 py-0.5 sm:py-1 bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 rounded text-xs font-semibold flex-shrink-0">
                                📦 {containerIds.length}
                              </span>
                            )}
                          </div>
                          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-4 text-xs sm:text-sm text-gray-600">
                            <span className="flex items-center">
                              <MapPin className="h-3 w-3 sm:h-4 sm:w-4 mr-1" />
                              {formatDistance(leg.actual_distance)}
                            </span>
                            <span className="flex items-center">
                              <Clock className="h-3 w-3 sm:h-4 sm:w-4 mr-1" />
                              {formatDuration(leg.travel_duration)}
                            </span>
                            {leg.average_speed && leg.average_speed > 0 && !isMobile && (
                              <span className="flex items-center">
                                <Gauge className="h-3 w-3 sm:h-4 sm:w-4 mr-1" />
                                {leg.average_speed.toFixed(1)} km/h
                              </span>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>

<div className="flex items-center space-x-2 sm:space-x-4 flex-shrink-0">
                        {leg.osrm_distance && leg.osrm_distance > 0 && !isMobile && (
                          <div className="text-right">
                            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">vs Optimal</p>
                            <p className={`text-sm font-semibold ${
                              (leg.actual_distance - leg.osrm_distance) <= 2 ? 'text-green-600' : 
                              (leg.actual_distance - leg.osrm_distance) <= 5 ? 'text-yellow-600' : 
                              'text-red-600'
                            }`}>
                              {leg.actual_distance > leg.osrm_distance ? '+' : ''}{(leg.actual_distance - leg.osrm_distance).toFixed(1)} km
                            </p>
                          </div>
                        )}
                        {isExpanded ? <ChevronUp className="h-4 w-4 sm:h-5 sm:w-5 text-gray-400" /> : <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 sm:h-5 sm:w-5 text-gray-400" />}
                      </div>
                    </button>

                    {isExpanded && (
                      <div className="px-3 sm:px-6 pb-4 sm:pb-6 pt-2">
                        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4 sm:p-5 shadow-sm">
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3 sm:gap-4 mb-4">
                            <div>
                              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">🕐 Departure</p>
                              <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">{formatTime(leg.departure_time)}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">🕑 Arrival</p>
                              <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">{formatTime(leg.arrival_time)}</p>
                            </div>
                            {leg.dwell_time > 0 && (
                              <div>
                                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">⏱️ Dwell Time</p>
                                <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">{formatDuration(leg.dwell_time)}</p>
                              </div>
                            )}
                            {leg.max_speed && leg.max_speed > 0 && (
                              <div>
                                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">🚀 Max Speed</p>
                                <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">{leg.max_speed.toFixed(1)} km/h</p>
                              </div>
                            )}
                          </div>

                          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3 sm:gap-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
                            <div>
                              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-2">📍 From Location</p>
                              <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded p-2 sm:p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 mb-1">{leg.from_name}</p>
                                <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 font-mono break-all">
                                  {leg.from_location_lat?.toFixed(6)}, {leg.from_location_lng?.toFixed(6)}
                                </p>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-2">📍 To Location</p>
                              <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded p-2 sm:p-3">
                                <p className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 mb-1">{leg.to_name}</p>
                                <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 font-mono break-all">
                                  {leg.to_location_lat?.toFixed(6)}, {leg.to_location_lng?.toFixed(6)}
                                </p>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </div>

                          {leg.osrm_distance && leg.osrm_distance > 0 && (
                            <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
                              <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3">📊 Route Comparison</p>
                              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 sm:gap-4">
                                <div className="bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-3 border border-blue-200">
                                  <p className="text-xs text-blue-600 mb-1 font-semibold">Actual Route</p>
                                  <p className="text-base sm:text-lg font-bold text-blue-900">{formatDistance(leg.actual_distance)}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs text-blue-600 mt-1">{formatDuration(leg.travel_duration)}</p>
                                </div>
                                <div className="bg-green-50 rounded-lg p-3 border border-green-200">
                                  <p className="text-xs text-green-600 mb-1 font-semibold">Optimal Route</p>
                                  <p className="text-base sm:text-lg font-bold text-green-900">{formatDistance(leg.osrm_distance)}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs text-green-600 mt-1">
                                    {tripData.OptimalLegs?.find(ol => ol.sequence_number === leg.sequence_number)?.travel_duration 
                                      ? formatDuration(tripData.OptimalLegs.find(ol => ol.sequence_number === leg.sequence_number).travel_duration)
                                      : 'N/A'}
                                  </p>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          )}

                          {!isReturnLeg && containerIds.length > 0 && (
                            <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
                              <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-2">📦 Container IDs</p>
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                                {containerIds.map(id => (
                                  <span key={id} className="px-2 sm:px-3 py-1 bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold border border-purple-200">
                                    #{id}
                                  </span>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default TripSummaryRouteView;
===== ./TripTable.tsx =====
import React, { useState, useMemo, useCallback } from "react";
import { Link } from "react-router-dom";
import {
  Edit3,
  FileText,
  Trash2,
  MapPin,
  User,
  Car,
  Fuel,
  DollarSign,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronRight,
  ChevronUp,
  Layers,
  FileCheck,
  Image as ImageIcon,
  X,
  Map,
  Calendar,
  Building2,
  Package,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock,
  Archive,
} from "lucide-react";
import TableHeader from "./TableHeader";
import EmptyTableState from "./EmptyTableState";
import { SERVER_IP } from "../../config";

// Types
interface ReceiptStep {
  ID?: number;
  location: string;
  stamped: boolean;
}

interface Receipt {
  ID: number;
  image_path: string;
}

interface ReceiptBatch {
  ID?: number;
  id?: number;
  status: string;
  receipts?: Receipt[];
}

interface ParentTrip {
  ID: number;
  car_id: number;
  driver_id: number;
  car_no_plate: string;
  driver_name: string;
  transporter: string;
  company: string;
  terminal: string;
  date: string;
  author?: string | null;
  overwriter?: string | null;
  receipt_batch?: ReceiptBatch;
  total_revenue?: number;
  total_containers?: number;
}

interface Location {
  ID: number;
  Name: string;
  latitude: string;
  longitude: string;
}

interface Trip {
  ID: number;
  CreatedAt: string;
  UpdatedAt: string;
  DeletedAt: string | null;
  parent_trip_id?: number;
  car_id: number;
  driver_id: number;
  car_no_plate: string;
  driver_name: string;
  transporter: string;
  tank_capacity: number;
  company: string;
  terminal: string;
  drop_off_point: string;
  location_name: string;
  capacity: number;
  gas_type: string;
  date: string;
  revenue: number;
  mileage: number;
  receipt_no: string;
  distance: number;
  fee: number;
  location: Location;
  parent_trip?: ParentTrip;
  receipt_steps: ReceiptStep[];
}

interface SortConfig {
  key: string | null;
  direction: "ascending" | "descending";
}

interface TripTableProps {
  isLoading: boolean;
  trips: Trip[];
  sortConfig: SortConfig;
  onSort: (key: string) => void;
  onDelete: (id: number) => void;
  onDeleteParent: (id: number, containerCount?: number) => void;
  onShowDetails: (id: number) => void;
  onManageReceipt: (id: number) => void;
}

const TripTable: React.FC<TripTableProps> = ({
  isLoading,
  trips,
  sortConfig,
  onSort,
  onDelete,
  onDeleteParent,
  onShowDetails,
  onManageReceipt,
}) => {
  const [expandedGroups, setExpandedGroups] = useState<Set<number>>(new Set());
  const [selectedReceiptBatch, setSelectedReceiptBatch] =
    useState<ReceiptBatch | null>(null);
  const [selectedImage, setSelectedImage] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Mobile state
  const [visibleDetailId, setVisibleDetailId] = useState<number | null>(null);

  // Memoized format functions
  const formatCurrency = useCallback((amount: number | undefined): string => {
    if (typeof amount !== "number") return String(amount || "—");
    return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", {
      minimumFractionDigits: 0,
      maximumFractionDigits: 0,
    }).format(amount);
  }, []);

  const formatDistance = useCallback((distance: number | undefined): string => {
    if (typeof distance !== "number") return String(distance || "—");
    return `${distance.toFixed(1)} km`;
  }, []);

  const formatDate = useCallback((dateString: string | undefined): string => {
    if (!dateString) return "—";
    try {
      return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString("en-US", {
        month: "short",
        day: "numeric",
        year: "numeric",
      });
    } catch {
      return dateString;
    }
  }, []);

  const truncateText = useCallback(
    (text: string | undefined, maxLength: number = 20): string => {
      if (!text) return "—";
      if (text.length <= maxLength) return text;
      return text.substring(0, maxLength) + "...";
    },
    []
  );

  const getImageUrl = useCallback((imagePath: string): string => {
    return `${SERVER_IP}/receipts/${imagePath}`;
  }, []);

  const getReceiptStatus = useCallback((trip: Trip) => {
    if (!trip.receipt_steps || trip.receipt_steps.length === 0) {
      return {
        status: "pending",
        label: "Pending",
        classes: "bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 border-gray-200",
        icon: Clock,
      };
    }

    const hasGarage = trip.receipt_steps.some((s) => s.location === "Garage");
    const hasOffice = trip.receipt_steps.some((s) => s.location === "Office");
    const isStamped = trip.receipt_steps.some((s) => s.stamped === true);

    if (hasGarage && hasOffice) {
      return {
        status: "complete",
        label: isStamped ? "Complete & Stamped" : "Complete",
        classes: isStamped
          ? "bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 border-emerald-200"
          : "bg-green-100 text-green-700 border-green-200",
        icon: CheckCircle2,
      };
    }

    if (hasGarage || hasOffice) {
      return {
        status: "in_progress",
        label: hasGarage ? "In Garage" : "In Office",
        classes: "bg-amber-100 text-amber-700 border-amber-200",
        icon: Archive,
      };
    }

    return {
      status: "pending",
      label: "Pending",
      classes: "bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 border-gray-200",
      icon: Clock,
    };
  }, []);

  const handleViewReceiptBatch = useCallback((parentTrip: ParentTrip) => {
    if (parentTrip?.receipt_batch) {
      setSelectedReceiptBatch(parentTrip.receipt_batch);
    }
  }, []);

  const toggleGroup = useCallback((parentId: number) => {
    setExpandedGroups((prev) => {
      const newExpanded = new Set(prev);
      if (newExpanded.has(parentId)) {
        newExpanded.delete(parentId);
      } else {
        newExpanded.add(parentId);
      }
      return newExpanded;
    });
  }, []);

  // Memoized trip grouping
  const displayItems = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped: { [key: number]: Trip[] } = {};
    const standalone: Trip[] = [];

    trips.forEach((trip) => {
      if (trip.parent_trip_id) {
        if (!grouped[trip.parent_trip_id]) {
          grouped[trip.parent_trip_id] = [];
        }
        grouped[trip.parent_trip_id].push(trip);
      } else {
        standalone.push(trip);
      }
    });

    const items: any[] = [];

    standalone.forEach((trip) => {
      items.push({ type: "standalone", trip });
    });

    Object.entries(grouped).forEach(([parentId, containers]) => {
      items.push({
        type: "parent",
        parentId: parseInt(parentId),
        containers,
        isExpanded: expandedGroups.has(parseInt(parentId)),
        parentTrip: containers[0]?.parent_trip,
      });
    });

    items.sort((a, b) => {
      const dateA =
        a.type === "standalone" ? a.trip.date : a.containers[0].date;
      const dateB =
        b.type === "standalone" ? b.trip.date : b.containers[0].date;
      return new Date(dateB).getTime() - new Date(dateA).getTime();
    });

    return items;
  }, [trips, expandedGroups]);

  if (isLoading && !trips.length) {
    return (
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-6 text-center">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
          <div className="w-6 h-6 border-2 border-blue-200 border-t-blue-600 rounded-full animate-spin mb-3"></div>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">Loading trips...</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (trips.length === 0) {
    return <EmptyTableState />;
  }

  return (
    <>
      {/* Desktop View */}
      <div className="hidden lg:block bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
        <div className="overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full min-w-[1200px]">
            <thead>
              <tr className="bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-50 to-gray-100 border-b border-gray-200">
                <th className="py-4 pl-6 pr-3 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider w-12">
                  {/* Expand column */}
                </th>
                <TableHeader
                  label="Receipt No / Type"
                  field="receipt_no"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="py-4 pl-3 pr-3 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Date"
                  field="date"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Company"
                  field="company"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Route"
                  field="terminal"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Vehicle & Driver"
                  field="car_no_plate"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Tank"
                  field="tank_capacity"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <TableHeader
                  label="Distance & Fee"
                  field="mileage"
                  sortConfig={sortConfig}
                  onSort={onSort}
                  className="px-3 py-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider"
                  icon={null}
                />
                <th className="px-6 py-4 text-right text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase tracking-wider">
                  Actions
                </th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody className="divide-y divide-gray-100">
              {isLoading && !trips.length ? (
                <tr>
                  <td colSpan={9} className="px-6 py-12 text-center">
                    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
                      <div className="w-8 h-8 border-3 border-blue-200 border-t-blue-600 rounded-full animate-spin mb-4"></div>
                      <p className="text-gray-500">Loading trips...</p>
                    </div>
                  </td>
                </tr>
              ) : (
                displayItems.map((item, index) => {
                  if (item.type === "standalone") {
                    const trip = item.trip;
                    return (
                      <tr
                        key={`standalone-${trip.ID}`}
                        className={`hover:bg-blue-50/50 transition-colors duration-150 ${
                          index % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/30"
                        }`}
                      >
                        <td className="py-4 pl-6 pr-3">
                          {/* Empty expand cell */}
                        </td>

                        {/* Receipt */}
                        <td className="py-4 pl-3 pr-3">
                          <div className="flex items-center">
                            <div className="flex-shrink-0">
                              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg bg-blue-100 flex items-center justify-center">
                                <FileText className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="ml-3">
                              <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">
                                #{trip.receipt_no || "N/A"}
                              </div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                                Single Trip
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Date */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                            {formatDate(trip.date)}
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Company */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div
                            className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 truncate max-w-[120px]"
                            title={trip.company}
                          >
                            {trip.company}
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Route */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div className="space-y-1">
                            <div className="flex items-center text-xs">
                              <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                              <span
                                className="text-gray-700 truncate"
                                style={{ direction: "ltr", textAlign: "left" }}
                                title={trip.terminal}
                              >
                                {trip.terminal}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center text-xs">
                              <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-red-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                              <span
                                className="text-gray-700 truncate"
                                style={{ direction: "ltr", textAlign: "left" }}
                                title={trip.drop_off_point}
                              >
                                {trip.drop_off_point}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Vehicle & Driver */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div className="space-y-2">
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <Car className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                              <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                                {trip.car_no_plate}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <div className="w-4 h-4 bg-gray-200 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mr-2 flex-shrink-0">
                                <User className="h-2.5 w-2.5 text-gray-500" />
                              </div>
                              <div
                                className="text-sm text-gray-700 truncate"
                                style={{ direction: "ltr", textAlign: "left" }}
                                title={trip.driver_name}
                              >
                                {trip.driver_name}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Tank */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div className="flex items-center">
                            <Fuel className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2" />
                            <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                              {trip.tank_capacity || "—"}L
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Distance & Fee */}
                        <td className="px-3 py-4">
                          <div className="space-y-1">
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                              <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">
                                {formatDistance(trip.mileage)}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                              <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-green-600">
                                {formatCurrency(trip.fee)}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>

                        {/* Actions */}
                        <td className="px-6 py-4 text-right">
                          <div className="flex items-center justify-end space-x-2">
                            <Link
                              to={`/trips/${trip.ID}`}
                              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-700 hover:bg-blue-100 transition-colors"
                              title="Edit Trip"
                            >
                              <Edit3 className="h-4 w-4" />
                            </Link>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => onShowDetails(trip.ID)}
                              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-green-600 hover:text-green-700 hover:bg-green-100 transition-colors"
                              title="View Details"
                            >
                              <FileText className="h-4 w-4" />
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => onManageReceipt(trip.ID)}
                              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-purple-600 hover:text-purple-700 hover:bg-purple-100 transition-colors"
                              title="Manage Receipt"
                            >
                              <FileCheck className="h-4 w-4" />
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => onDelete(trip.ID)}
                              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-red-600 hover:text-red-700 hover:bg-red-100 transition-colors"
                              title="Delete Trip"
                            >
                              <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                            </button>
                          </div>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    );
                  } else {
                    // Parent group
                    const containers = item.containers;
                    const firstContainer = containers[0];
                    const parentTrip = item.parentTrip;
                    const totalCapacity = containers.reduce(
                      (sum: number, c: Trip) => sum + c.tank_capacity,
                      0
                    );
                    const isExpanded = item.isExpanded;
                    const hasMultipleContainers = containers.length > 1;
                    const hasReceiptBatch = item.parentTrip?.receipt_batch;

                    return (
                      <React.Fragment key={`parent-${item.parentId}`}>
                        {/* Parent Row */}
                        <tr
                          className={`hover:bg-blue-50/50 transition-colors duration-150 ${
                            index % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/30"
                          }`}
                        >
                          <td className="py-4 pl-6 pr-3">
                            <button
                              onClick={() => toggleGroup(item.parentId)}
                              className="p-1 hover:bg-blue-100 rounded transition-colors"
                            >
                              {isExpanded ? (
                                <ChevronDown className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                              ) : (
                                <ChevronRight className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                              )}
                            </button>
                          </td>

                          {/* Type indicator */}
                          <td className="py-4 pl-3 pr-3">
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <div className="flex-shrink-0">
                                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg bg-purple-100 flex items-center justify-center relative">
                                  <Layers className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-600" />
                                  {hasReceiptBatch && (
                                    <div
                                      className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 bg-orange-500 rounded-full border-2 border-white"
                                      title="Has receipt batch"
                                    ></div>
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <div className="ml-3">
                                <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">
                                  #{parentTrip.ID}
                                </div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                                  {containers.length} Containers
                                  {hasReceiptBatch && (
                                    <span className="ml-1 text-orange-600">
                                      • Has receipts
                                    </span>
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Date */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                              {formatDate(firstContainer.date)}
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Company */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div
                              className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 truncate max-w-[120px]"
                              title={firstContainer.company}
                            >
                              {firstContainer.company}
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Route */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div className="space-y-1">
                              <div className="flex items-center text-xs">
                                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                                <span
                                  className="text-gray-700 truncate"
                                  title={firstContainer.terminal}
                                >
                                  {firstContainer.terminal}
                                </span>
                              </div>
                              <div className="flex items-center text-xs">
                                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-purple-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                                <span className="text-gray-700">
                                  {containers.length} destinations
                                </span>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Vehicle & Driver */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div className="space-y-2">
                              <div className="flex items-center">
                                <Car className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                                <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                                  {firstContainer.car_no_plate}
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <div className="flex items-center">
                                <div className="w-4 h-4 bg-gray-200 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mr-2 flex-shrink-0">
                                  <User className="h-2.5 w-2.5 text-gray-500" />
                                </div>
                                <div className="text-sm text-gray-700 truncate">
                                  {firstContainer.driver_name}
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Total Tank */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div className="flex items-center">
                              <Fuel className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2" />
                              <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                                {totalCapacity}L
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">
                              Total
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Summary */}
                          <td className="px-3 py-4">
                            <div className="text-xs text-purple-600 font-medium">
                              {isExpanded ? "View less" : "View containers"}
                            </div>
                          </td>

                          {/* Actions for parent */}
                          <td className="px-6 py-4 text-right">
                            <div className="flex items-center justify-end space-x-2">
                              <Link
                                to={`/trips/multi-container/${item.parentId}/edit`}
                                className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-700 hover:bg-blue-100 transition-colors"
                                title="Edit Multi-Container Trip"
                              >
                                <Edit3 className="h-4 w-4" />
                              </Link>
                              {firstContainer.company === "Watanya" && (
                                <Link
                                  to={`/trips/parent/${item.parentId}/route-summary`}
                                  className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-indigo-600 hover:text-indigo-700 hover:bg-indigo-100 transition-colors"
                                  title="View Route Summary"
                                >
                                  <Map className="h-4 w-4" />
                                </Link>
                              )}
                              {hasReceiptBatch && (
                                <button
                                  onClick={() =>
                                    handleViewReceiptBatch(item.parentTrip)
                                  }
                                  className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-700 hover:bg-orange-100 transition-colors"
                                  title="View Receipt Batch"
                                >
                                  <ImageIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                                </button>
                              )}
                              <button
                                onClick={() =>
                                  onDeleteParent(
                                    item.parentId,
                                    containers.length
                                  )
                                }
                                className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-red-600 hover:text-red-700 hover:bg-red-100 transition-colors"
                                title="Delete Multi-Container Trip"
                              >
                                <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                              </button>
                              <button
                                onClick={() => toggleGroup(item.parentId)}
                                className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-purple-600 hover:text-purple-700 hover:bg-purple-100 transition-colors"
                                title={isExpanded ? "Collapse" : "Expand"}
                              >
                                {isExpanded ? (
                                  <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4" />
                                ) : (
                                  <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
                                )}
                              </button>
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>

                        {/* Author and Overwriter Row - only show if they exist */}
                        {isExpanded &&
                          parentTrip &&
                          (parentTrip.author || parentTrip.overwriter) && (
                            <tr className="bg-purple-50/30">
                              <td colSpan={9} className="px-6 py-2">
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs pl-14">
                                  {parentTrip.author && (
                                    <div className="flex items-center">
                                      <User className="h-3 w-3 text-purple-600 mr-1.5" />
                                      <span className="text-purple-700 font-medium">
                                        Author:
                                      </span>
                                      <span className="text-purple-900 ml-1">
                                        {parentTrip.author}
                                      </span>
                                    </div>
                                  )}
                                  {parentTrip.overwriter && (
                                    <div className="flex items-center">
                                      <Edit3 className="h-3 w-3 text-purple-600 mr-1.5" />
                                      <span className="text-purple-700 font-medium">
                                        Overwriter:
                                      </span>
                                      <span className="text-purple-900 ml-1">
                                        {parentTrip.overwriter}
                                      </span>
                                    </div>
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          )}

                        {/* Container Rows (when expanded) */}
                        {isExpanded &&
                          containers.map(
                            (container: Trip, containerIndex: number) => (
                              <tr
                                key={`container-${container.ID}`}
                                className="bg-purple-50/30 hover:bg-purple-50/50 transition-colors"
                              >
                                <td className="py-3 pl-6 pr-3">
                                  <div className="w-px h-8 bg-purple-200 ml-2"></div>
                                </td>

                                {/* Receipt with indent */}
                                <td className="py-3 pl-3 pr-3">
                                  <div className="flex items-center pl-6">
                                    <div className="flex-shrink-0">
                                      <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-white border-2 border-purple-200 flex items-center justify-center">
                                        <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-purple-600">
                                          {containerIndex + 1}
                                        </span>
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div className="ml-3">
                                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                                        #{container.receipt_no}
                                      </div>
                                      <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                                        Container {containerIndex + 1}
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                </td>

                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  {/* Empty - date is same for all */}
                                </td>

                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  {/* Empty - company is same for all */}
                                </td>

                                {/* Route - show drop-off point */}
                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  <div className="flex items-center text-xs pl-4">
                                    <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-red-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                                    <span className="text-gray-700">
                                      {container.drop_off_point}
                                    </span>
                                  </div>
                                </td>

                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  {/* Empty - vehicle is same for all */}
                                </td>

                                {/* Container capacity */}
                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  <div className="flex items-center">
                                    <Fuel className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2" />
                                    <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                                      {container.tank_capacity}L
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                </td>

                                {/* Distance & Fee */}
                                <td className="px-3 py-3">
                                  <div className="space-y-1">
                                    <div className="flex items-center">
                                      <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900">
                                        {formatDistance(container.mileage)}
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div className="flex items-center">
                                      <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500 mr-2 flex-shrink-0" />
                                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-green-600">
                                        {formatCurrency(container.fee)}
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                </td>

                                {/* Actions for container */}
                                <td className="px-6 py-3 text-right">
                                  <div className="flex items-center justify-end space-x-2">
                                    <button
                                      onClick={() =>
                                        onShowDetails(container.ID)
                                      }
                                      className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-green-600 hover:text-green-700 hover:bg-green-100 transition-colors"
                                      title="View Details"
                                    >
                                      <FileText className="h-4 w-4" />
                                    </button>
                                    <button
                                      onClick={() =>
                                        onManageReceipt(container.ID)
                                      }
                                      className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-purple-600 hover:text-purple-700 hover:bg-purple-100 transition-colors"
                                      title="Manage Receipt"
                                    >
                                      <FileCheck className="h-4 w-4" />
                                    </button>
                                    {hasMultipleContainers && (
                                      <button
                                        onClick={() => onDelete(container.ID)}
                                        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-8 rounded-lg text-red-600 hover:text-red-700 hover:bg-red-100 transition-colors"
                                        title="Delete Container"
                                      >
                                        <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                                      </button>
                                    )}
                                  </div>
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                            )
                          )}
                      </React.Fragment>
                    );
                  }
                })
              )}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Mobile View */}
      <div className="block lg:hidden">
        {displayItems.map((item) => {
          if (item.type === "standalone") {
            const trip = item.trip;
            const receiptStatus = getReceiptStatus(trip);
            const StatusIcon = receiptStatus.icon;

            return (
              <div
                key={`mobile-trip-${trip.ID}`}
                className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden mb-3"
              >
                <div
                  className="p-4 cursor-pointer"
                  onClick={() =>
                    setVisibleDetailId(
                      visibleDetailId === trip.ID ? null : trip.ID
                    )
                  }
                >
                  {/* Header */}
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                      <FileText className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                      <span className="font-bold text-gray-900">
                        #{trip.receipt_no}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                      <span
                        className={`inline-flex items-center px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium border ${receiptStatus.classes}`}
                      >
                        <StatusIcon className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                        {receiptStatus.label}
                      </span>
                      {visibleDetailId === trip.ID ? (
                        <ChevronUp className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                      ) : (
                        <ChevronDown className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Basic Info Grid */}
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
                    <div className="flex items-center">
                      <Calendar className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-2" />
                      <span className="text-gray-600">
                        {formatDate(trip.date)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center">
                      <Building2 className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-500 mr-2" />
                      <span className="font-semibold text-gray-900">
                        {truncateText(trip.company, 15)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Route */}
                  <div className="mt-3 space-y-1">
                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm">
                      <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                      <span className="text-gray-600">
                        {truncateText(trip.terminal, 25)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm">
                      <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-red-500 rounded-full mr-2"></div>
                      <span className="text-gray-700 font-medium">
                        {truncateText(trip.drop_off_point, 25)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Vehicle and Metrics */}
                  <div className="mt-3 flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
                    <div className="flex items-center">
                      <Car className="h-4 w-4 text-gray-400 mr-1.5" />
                      <span className="font-semibold text-gray-900">
                        {trip.car_no_plate}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-indigo-500 mr-1" />
                        <span className="font-bold text-indigo-600">
                          {formatDistance(trip.mileage)}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-500 mr-1" />
                        <span className="font-bold text-emerald-600">
                          {formatCurrency(trip.fee)}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Expanded Details */}
                {visibleDetailId === trip.ID && (
                  <div className="border-t border-gray-100 p-4 space-y-3 bg-gray-50">
                    {/* Driver Info */}
                    <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border border-gray-200">
                      <div className="flex items-center mb-2">
                        <User className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-500 mr-2" />
                        <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-500 uppercase">
                          Driver
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <p className="text-sm text-gray-900">
                        {trip.driver_name}
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    {/* Tank Capacity */}
                    <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border border-gray-200">
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <div className="flex items-center">
                          <Fuel className="h-4 w-4 text-orange-500 mr-2" />
                          <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-500 uppercase">
                            Tank
                          </span>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-900">
                          {trip.tank_capacity}L
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Receipt Tracking */}
                    {trip.receipt_steps && trip.receipt_steps.length > 0 && (
                      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border border-gray-200">
                        <div className="flex items-center mb-2">
                          <Archive className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-500 mr-2" />
                          <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-500 uppercase">
                            Receipt
                          </span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="space-y-2">
                          {trip.receipt_steps.map((step, idx) => (
                            <div
                              key={idx}
                              className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm"
                            >
                              <div className="flex items-center">
                                <CheckCircle2
                                  className={`h-3.5 w-3.5 mr-2 ${
                                    step.stamped
                                      ? "text-emerald-500"
                                      : "text-blue-500"
                                  }`}
                                />
                                <span className="font-medium text-gray-700">
                                  {step.location}
                                </span>
                              </div>
                              {step.stamped && (
                                <span className="inline-flex items-center px-2 py-0.5 rounded bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 font-semibold text-xs">
                                  Stamped
                                </span>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {/* Action Buttons */}
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                      <Link
                        to={`/trips/${trip.ID}`}
                        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-3 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors font-medium text-sm"
                      >
                        <Edit3 className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5" />
                        Edit
                      </Link>

                      <button
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          onShowDetails(trip.ID);
                        }}
                        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-3 py-2 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-indigo-700 transition-colors font-medium text-sm"
                      >
                        <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5" />
                        Map
                      </button>

                      <button
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          onManageReceipt(trip.ID);
                        }}
                        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-3 py-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-700 transition-colors font-medium text-sm"
                      >
                        <FileCheck className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5" />
                        Receipt
                      </button>

                      <button
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          onDelete(trip.ID);
                        }}
                        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-3 py-2 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-red-700 transition-colors font-medium text-sm"
                      >
                        <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5" />
                        Delete
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            );
          } else {
            // Parent group mobile view
            const containers = item.containers;
            const parentTrip = item.parentTrip;
            const hasMultipleContainers = containers.length > 1;
            const totalRevenue = containers.reduce(
              (sum: number, c: Trip) => sum + (c.fee || 0),
              0
            );
            const totalDistance = containers.reduce(
              (sum: number, c: Trip) => sum + (c.mileage || 0),
              0
            );
            const hasReceiptBatch = parentTrip?.receipt_batch;

            return (
              <div
                key={`mobile-parent-${item.parentId}`}
                className="bg-gradient-to-br from-white to-blue-50 rounded-lg shadow-md border-2 border-blue-200 overflow-hidden mb-3"
              >
                <div
                  className="p-4 cursor-pointer"
                  onClick={() => toggleGroup(item.parentId)}
                >
                  {/* Header */}
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                      <Layers className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-700" />
                      <div>
                        <span className="font-bold text-purple-900">
                          #{parentTrip.ID}
                        </span>
                        <p className="text-xs text-purple-600 mt-0.5">
                          {containers.length} container
                          {containers.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""}
                          {hasReceiptBatch && (
                            <span className="ml-1 text-orange-600">
                              • Has receipts
                            </span>
                          )}
                        </p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                      {hasReceiptBatch && (
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleViewReceiptBatch(parentTrip);
                          }}
                          className="p-1.5 bg-orange-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-orange-600 transition-colors"
                        >
                          <ImageIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
                        </button>
                      )}
                      {item.isExpanded ? (
                        <ChevronUp className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-700" />
                      ) : (
                        <ChevronDown className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-700" />
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Basic Info Grid */}
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
                    <div className="flex items-center">
                      <Calendar className="h-4 w-4 text-purple-600 mr-2" />
                      <span className="text-purple-800 font-medium">
                        {formatDate(containers[0].date)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center">
                      <Building2 className="h-4 w-4 text-purple-700 mr-2" />
                      <span className="font-bold text-purple-900">
                        {truncateText(containers[0].company, 15)}
                      </span>
